    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });

Can Mike survive his unsolicited undercover work and cleanse his sullied reputation? Or will he end up as shark bait for double-crossing the wrong people?</span>

<div id="review_3109051353" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3109051353" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3109051353?book_show_action=true">Dec 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3109051353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16875388885422180701">One exceptionally fine thriller!<br/><br/>California author Mark Barkawitz is a screenwriter, actor, creative writing teacher, athlete and track coach whose fiction, essays, poetry and screenwriting have won multiple awards. His books to date include GIANT KILLERS, THE DOG WITH THE OPPOSABLE THUMB, 29 AGAIN AND OTHER CANCER-FIGHTING STORIES, and now FULL MOON SATURDAY NIGHT. In addition to his many literary accomplishments, Mark is a cancer survivor whose indomitable spirit has influenced many with critic</span>
  <span id="freeText16875388885422180701" style="display:none">One exceptionally fine thriller!<br /><br />California author Mark Barkawitz is a screenwriter, actor, creative writing teacher, athlete and track coach whose fiction, essays, poetry and screenwriting have won multiple awards. His books to date include GIANT KILLERS, THE DOG WITH THE OPPOSABLE THUMB, 29 AGAIN AND OTHER CANCER-FIGHTING STORIES, and now FULL MOON SATURDAY NIGHT. In addition to his many literary accomplishments, Mark is a cancer survivor whose indomitable spirit has influenced many with critical illnesses as well as bringing support to the City of Hope research and patient care. He lives in Pasadena, California. <br /><br />Perhaps Mark’s skills, outlined in brief above, gained in screenwriting and in dealing with the ‘wages of life,’ are in part responsible for this exceptionally fine thriller. But whatever the nidus for his talent, this new novel places him solidly in the forefront of contemporary fiction authors. He is able to convey a breathlessly paced mystery while peppering it with a wry humor that serves to make his prose unique.<br /><br />A sample of Mark’s talent opens his story – ‘When our dates for the party excused themselves to use the bathroom, I took advantage of their absence and leaned closer to Cooper with his back to the wall. “Just so we’re straight,” I said confidentially, staring into his lazy eyes, a stupid smile on his sophomoric, look-I-can-grow-a-mustache-now face. “I don’t like you.” “What?” He seemed truly shocked by my candor. He was young, dumb, and handsome, dating my ex-girlfriend Mandy with eyes for my current girlfriend Marie. It was a small party: mostly undergrads from the state college from which I’d recently graduated and others. The music was loud, so no one appeared to take notice of my confrontation. “Why-why not, Mike?” He took a slug of his apple beer – clueless…’<br /><br />Once the principal character Mike has been defined, the story revs up, and the plot unfolds – ‘Mike Hepp is an L.A. millennial post-grad, who dreams of making it big in the TV &amp; film industry. He auditions by day and tends bar at night to satiate his massive student debt, credit card payments, and rent. Until one knuckle-busting, full moon Saturday night launches his life into complete upheaval, suddenly placing him in the middle of an international drug smuggling operation and an undercover police sting, consequently ruining his reputation in Hollywood. Can Mike survive his unsolicited undercover work and cleanse his sullied reputation? Or will he end up as shark bait for double-crossing the wrong people?’ Truth – and consequences, and the velocity of the action is way past the speed limit.<br /><br />It is not often a book can be stamped “brilliant” but novel meets the criteria! Very highly recommended. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16875388885422180701" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText13251636990193587181" style="display:none">Full Moon Saturday Night by Mark Barkawitz<br />Book starts out with Mike, working weekends at the bar and writing scenes for a tv show. <div id="review_3088543220" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3088543220" />
    <a title="Ground Breaking" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/106915444-ground-breaking"><img alt="Ground Breaking" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576584734p2/106915444.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3088543220?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ground Breaking" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ground Breaking" href="/user/show/106915444-ground-breaking">Ground Breaking</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3088543220" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17803847704489477184">If you're looking for a new thriller novel to read, then look no further than 'Full Moon Saturday Night' by Mark Barkawitz. The plot is unique and contemporary, with many unexpected twists and turns that gave me no idea what might happen next. This makes 'Full Moon Saturday Night' a really quick read as I just had to read 'one more chapter' before I could put it down.<br/><br/>Mike is an aspiring actor, getting nowhere in his career and racking up the debt. He is treading water, until one night everything</span>
  <span id="freeText17803847704489477184" style="display:none">If you're looking for a new thriller novel to read, then look no further than 'Full Moon Saturday Night' by Mark Barkawitz. The plot is unique and contemporary, with many unexpected twists and turns that gave me no idea what might happen next. This makes 'Full Moon Saturday Night' a really quick read as I just had to read 'one more chapter' before I could put it down.<br /><br />Mike is an aspiring actor, getting nowhere in his career and racking up the debt. He is treading water, until one night everything changes, and he is thrown into the shady world of drug lords and police stings. Not only is his career as an actor on the line, but so is his life – you don't double-cross an international drug ring and just get to walk away.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17803847704489477184" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3631415232" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3631415232" />
    <a title="Pegboard" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard"><img alt="Pegboard" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498516338p2/47722544.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3631415232?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pegboard" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pegboard" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard">Pegboard</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3631415232" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7398054645685185073">Full Moon Saturday Night by Mark Barkawitz takes you to the world of a hopeful screen writer who lives in L.A. Mike Hepp works in a bar on nights so he can write and audition during the day. He doesn't get very far as ever step in the door leads to a dead end. Cornered into work for the police as an informant, Mike uses his contacts at the bar to get a female detective closer to the action. This causes problems with his friend since he can't tell anyone his secret. So many factors come into play</span>
  <span id="freeText7398054645685185073" style="display:none">Full Moon Saturday Night by Mark Barkawitz takes you to the world of a hopeful screen writer who lives in L.A. Mike Hepp works in a bar on nights so he can write and audition during the day. He doesn't get very far as ever step in the door leads to a dead end. Cornered into work for the police as an informant, Mike uses his contacts at the bar to get a female detective closer to the action. This causes problems with his friend since he can't tell anyone his secret. So many factors come into play and Mike wonders if he will lose his reputation in the world of Hollywood, his job, and his girlfriend.<br /><br />I found Mark Barkawitz a fascinating author who makes you feel as if you are right there with Mike. The plot appears simple at first, and then fans out into multiple twists of characters and activity. The characters were colorful, with interesting personalities. Overall, I was glued to the pages as Mike continues to hope when he faces many obstacles. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7398054645685185073" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

From there, the book just lot touch with reality.<br/><br/>It was a "page turner" for the first 3/4 of the book - but the last 1/4 just ruined it for me.<br/><br/>There are better reads out there in this genre.</span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('v6Jm/newsy/q/nGGhHxvUwqddanBCQXiwNZ22lojOYKFhA8szO56R03VxedziWWM3MKSYQ+Ei4WbqDBrl2DLGA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WL/MUqoX5SdqMpfYVpCqIbEtvpLROrDAR6EF6s1p7/RimaWAEUksT80ZI7mhZaD+Z3JZWh+3Pqcc30NbACodbg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer730353716466086648">Mark Barkawitz has earned local and national awards for his fiction, poetry, essay, and screenwriting. His work has appeared in newspapers, magazines, literary journals and anthologies, ‘zines, and on dozens of websites. He has IMDb feature film credits as screenwriter, actor, & associate producer (Mark Bark) for “Turn of the Blade” (NorthStar Ent.) and supporting actor in “The Killing Time” (New </span>
  <span id="freeText730353716466086648" style="display:none">Mark Barkawitz has earned local and national awards for his fiction, poetry, essay, and screenwriting. His work has appeared in newspapers, magazines, literary journals and anthologies, ‘zines, and on dozens of websites. He has IMDb feature film credits as screenwriter, actor, &amp; associate producer (Mark Bark) for “Turn of the Blade” (NorthStar Ent.) and supporting actor in “The Killing Time” (New World Pictures). He’s taught creative writing classes, coached a championship track team of student/athletes, and ran the 2001 L.A. Marathon in 3:44:42. He lives with his wife and has two kids in Pasadena, CA.</span>
